[37mRolling around a stretch of tall stones, the waters of the Modi River crash with[0m
[37ma powerful current, tossing up white spray in all directions. Fish swim through [0m
[37mthe waters, though their numbers are few, and the occasional frog hops up onto [0m
[37mthe rocks before being swept along in the water. Sturdy reeds manage to hold a [0m
[37mtenuous grasp on the riverbed, their stems bending in the current.[36m Silent and [0m
[36mobservant, a red fox stands here, alertly watching all with a cunning glint of [0m
[36mthe eye. Nervously pacing, a small brown lemming scampers under your feet. A [0m
[36mraven the colour of night perches nearby and observes curiously with beady black[0m
[36meyes. A grumpy badger stands here, snuffling about angrily. Fluttering on [0m
[36mdelicate wings, a huge gossamer butterfly flits about the room. Hackles raised, [0m
[36man adult grey wolf sniffs the air for enemies. Kioto, the Ancestor Dragon is [0m
[36mhere, with glowing eyes. A mule stands stubbornly, hooves planted solidly in the[0m
